---

# FAUNA | FLORA Docs

FAUNA is an AI agent that lives inside the FLORA canvas. Instead of manually dragging nodes, picking models, writing prompts, and building workflows - you describe what you want and FAUNA builds it.

It's not a chatbot. It has hands. It reads your canvas, adds nodes, chooses models, connects pipelines, runs generations, and organizes the output - all from a conversation.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#getting-started)

Getting Started

Open FAUNA by pressing `⌘ /` or `Ctrl /` anywhere on your canvas. A sidebar will appear on the right side, ready for your prompt.

You can also open FAUNA from the FAUNA button in the bottom-right corner of your canvas.

circle-info

**Quick tip:** Select nodes on your canvas before prompting - they'll automatically be included as context for FAUNA. You can also type `@` in the chat to mention specific nodes by name.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#what-fauna-can-do)

What FAUNA Can Do

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#chat-interface)

Chat interface

FAUNA is a full conversational agent - not a one-shot prompt box. You can have back-and-forth conversations, iterate on ideas, and build up complex workflows through dialogue.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#switch-modes)

Switch modes

FAUNA supports three modes of operation, selectable from the mode selector in the chat input:

*   **Assist mode** (default): FAUNA asks for your explicit confirmation before running any generations. You'll see which nodes it plans to execute and the estimated credit cost before anything runs.
    
*   **Auto mode**: FAUNA auto-runs all generations without pausing for approval. Best for when you want maximum speed.
    
*   **Plan mode**: FAUNA ideates on workflows but doesn't run anything. It only has access to information tools in this mode - useful when you want to focus on creative direction and structure before executing.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#generate-workflows-from-scratch)

Generate workflows from scratch

Describe what you want to create, and FAUNA will build the workflow for you - selecting appropriate models, configuring nodes, and connecting everything together.

**Try prompts like:**

*   "Generate a minimalist logo for a streetwear brand, create 3 campaign poster variations, then mock up the best one on a billboard and animate it into a 5-second video."
    
*   "Storyboard a 4-frame car commercial driving through a desert at sunset, then animate the hero frame into video."
    
*   "Generate a cinematic portrait, then create 4 art direction variations - film noir, golden hour, cyberpunk neon, and vintage Polaroid."
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#starter-prompts)

Starter prompts

When you first open FAUNA, you'll see quick action buttons to help you get started:

*   **What's new in FLORA** - Get up-to-date information about the latest FLORA features
    
*   **How does FLORA work?** - Learn about FLORA's capabilities
    
*   **What are the best models?** - Get model recommendations for your use case
    
*   **Create a starter workflow** - FAUNA generates a multi-step workflow you can customize
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#work-with-your-existing-canvas)

Work with your existing canvas

Select any nodes on your canvas, and FAUNA can:

*   Add new nodes that connect to your selection
    
*   Modify settings, labels, prompts, models, or aspect ratios
    
*   Reconnect or restructure your workflow
    
*   Remove nodes individually or by type
    
*   Create variations of existing nodes
    
*   Extend your workflow with additional steps
    
*   Group related nodes into containers
    
*   Arrange and organize nodes on your canvas
    

**Try prompts like:**

*   "Create 5 variants of this image"
    
*   "Change all the image nodes to use Ideogram 3.0"
    
*   "Connect these outputs to a new video node"
    
*   "Add an upscaling step after each image"
    
*   "Remove all the empty nodes"
    
*   "Group these image nodes together as 'Hero Shots'"
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#upload-images)

Upload images

You can attach images directly in the FAUNA chat to use as reference or source material. FAUNA supports:

*   **Drag and drop** images into the chat input
    
*   **Paste** images from your clipboard
    
*   **Click the attachment button** to select files
    

Accepted formats: JPEG, PNG, WebP, and GIF (up to 20 MB per file, maximum 5 attachments per message). FAUNA can place attached images onto your canvas as source nodes for other generation nodes to use.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#run-your-work)

Run your work

FAUNA can execute image, video, and text nodes - up to 50 at a time. Ask it to run specific nodes or entire sections of your workflow.

circle-info

**Approval required (in Assist mode):** When FAUNA wants to run nodes, it will show you which nodes it plans to execute and the estimated credit cost. You must approve before any generation runs - FAUNA won't spend your credits without your explicit confirmation. In Auto mode, FAUNA runs generations immediately.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#context-about-flora)

Context about FLORA

FAUNA has access to FLORA's documentation and model library. It knows every node type, every model, prompting best practices, and cost/quality tradeoffs. When you ask it to build or run something, it looks up:

*   How specific nodes work
    
*   Which models are available and what they're good at
    
*   Best practices for prompting different models
    
*   What's new in FLORA
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#the-sidebar)

The Sidebar

FAUNA lives in a sidebar on the right side of your canvas. It has two layout modes:

*   **Floating** - The sidebar overlays your canvas as a panel in the bottom-right corner
    
*   **Docked** - The sidebar attaches to the right edge of your screen at full height
    

Toggle between docked and floating with `⌘ \` (Mac) or `Ctrl \`.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#keyboard-shortcuts)

Keyboard Shortcuts

Shortcut

Action

`⌘ /` (Mac) or `Ctrl /`

Toggle FAUNA sidebar open/close

`⌘ \` (Mac) or `Ctrl \`

Toggle FAUNA sidebar between docked (right edge) and floating

`Escape`

Cancel pending execution if there is one, otherwise close the sidebar

`⌘ Enter` (Mac) or `Ctrl Enter`

When there's a pending execution, approve/continue

`Enter`

Send message

`Shift Enter`

New line in chat input

`@`

Open node picker to mention a specific canvas node

circle-info

Modifier keys are platform-aware - Mac shows `⌘` and Windows/Linux shows `Ctrl`.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#providing-context)

Providing Context

There are three ways to give FAUNA context about what you're working with:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#id-1.-select-nodes-on-your-canvas)

1\. Select nodes on your canvas

When you select nodes on the canvas, they're automatically included as context in your next message. This is the easiest and most common way to give FAUNA context.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#id-2.-use-mentions)

2\. Use @ mentions

Type `@` in the chat input to open a node picker. Search by node name or type, then select the node you want to reference. This is useful when you want to reference a specific node without selecting it on the canvas.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#id-3.-upload-images)

3\. Upload images

Attach images via drag-and-drop, paste, or the attachment button to use as reference material or source images.

circle-info

You can include up to 15 nodes as context in a single message.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#thinking-and-reasoning)

Thinking & Reasoning

FAUNA shows you its thinking process as it works. While FAUNA is processing your request, you'll see:

*   **A real-time shimmer indicator** showing what FAUNA is currently doing (e.g., "Reading canvas...", "Adding nodes...")
    
*   **An expandable thinking timeline** - after FAUNA responds, click "View steps" to see the full reasoning process, including which tools it used and what decisions it made
    

This transparency helps you understand FAUNA's approach and makes it easier to course-correct if needed.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#agentic-collaboration)

Agentic Collaboration

FAUNA works as an agent that does the work for you on canvas, not as a chat assistant. Think of it as a creative co-pilot that operates the tool for you - the closest analogy is Cursor for code.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#real-time-streaming)

Real-time streaming

As FAUNA thinks through your request, you'll see its responses stream in real-time. You can watch as it reasons through the problem, decides which tools to use, and takes action on your canvas.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#cancel-anytime)

Cancel anytime

Changed your mind? You can cancel FAUNA's response mid-stream if you see it going in a direction you don't want. Your conversation context is preserved, so you can immediately try a different approach.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#give-feedback)

Give feedback

You can rate FAUNA's responses with thumbs up or thumbs down on any assistant message. This feedback helps us improve FAUNA's performance over time.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#memory-and-sessions)

Memory & Sessions

FAUNA remembers your conversation history within each project. When you return to a project, you can pick up where you left off.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#how-memory-works)

How memory works

*   **Per-project sessions:** Each project has its own FAUNA session with its own conversation history
    
*   **Persistent messages:** Your messages and FAUNA's responses are saved automatically
    
*   **Context preserved:** The nodes you referenced in previous messages are tracked alongside the conversation
    
*   **Session history:** Access previous chat sessions from the dropdown in the sidebar header
    
*   **Rename sessions:** Give your sessions descriptive names by renaming them from the session dropdown
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#starting-fresh)

Starting fresh

If you want to start a new conversation without previous context, you can begin a new session using the new chat button in the top right corner of the sidebar header. Your previous session history remains accessible from the session dropdown.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#current-limitations)

Current Limitations

FAUNA is powerful but still has boundaries. Here's what to expect:

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#single-project-scope)

Single-project scope

FAUNA can only see and work with the project you currently have open. It can't access other projects, workspaces, or external websites.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#no-access-to-generation-history-or-past-assets)

No access to generation history or past assets

FAUNA doesn't yet have access to your existing project context, generation history, or assets from previous sessions.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#coming-soon)

Coming Soon

*   **Generate across projects** - Pull assets and context from other projects, not just the one you have open.
    
*   **Pull from your context** - FAUNA will have access to your existing project context, generation history, and past assets.
    
*   **Multiple FAUNA agents** - Run multiple agents and threads at the same time, so you can direct a team of creatives working in parallel.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#tips-for-better-results)

Tips for Better Results

circle-check

**Start small, then scale up.** Begin with simple tasks - changing a model, editing a prompt, or creating a single node. As you get comfortable, try larger requests like building workflow sections or running batch operations. This helps you learn FAUNA's strengths and discover how far you can push it.

**Be specific about your creative intent.** "Generate a cinematic product shot workflow for luxury watches" will get better results than "make something cool."

**Select relevant context.** Select nodes on your canvas before prompting, or use `@` to mention specific nodes. The more relevant context you provide, the better FAUNA understands what you're trying to do.

**Upload reference images.** Drag and drop or paste images directly into the chat to give FAUNA visual reference material for your creative direction.

**Iterate in conversation.** FAUNA works well when you build on previous responses. Start with a base workflow, then refine: "Now add a step that upscales the final output" or "Change the style to be more minimal."

**Review before running.** When in Assist mode, take a moment to review the node list and credit estimate before approving. This helps you stay in control of your usage.

**Reference nodes.** FAUNA can find nodes by their label, type, content, or model. For example: "make my image nodes use Ideogram 3.0" or "change all the Flux nodes to landscape format."

**Correct course when needed.** If you see FAUNA heading in the wrong direction, press Escape to stop it mid-response. Then tell it what went wrong and how to adjust - FAUNA learns from your feedback within the conversation.

**Start fresh when switching context.** When you're moving to a completely different part of your project or changing topics entirely, use the new chat button in the sidebar header. This clears the conversation history so FAUNA isn't confused by unrelated context from your previous work.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#we-want-your-feedback)

We Want Your Feedback

We're always learning how people want to use FAUNA. What's working? What's frustrating? What do you wish it could do?

**To share feedback:**

*   Rate responses with thumbs up/down directly in the chat
    
*   Fill out this short survey: [https://tally.so/r/XxJboLarrow-up-right](https://tally.so/r/XxJboL)
    

Specific examples help us most - if something didn't work as expected, tell us what you tried and what happened. If something worked great, we want to hear that too.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/fauna#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting

**FAUNA isn't responding.** Try closing and reopening the sidebar. If the issue persists, refresh your browser.

**FAUNA seems confused about my canvas.** Make sure you've selected the specific nodes you want it to work with, or use `@` mentions to reference them. FAUNA works best with explicit context rather than trying to understand your entire canvas at once.

**FAUNA made changes I didn't want.** Use undo (Cmd/Ctrl + Z) to reverse any canvas changes FAUNA made. You can also cancel a response mid-stream if you see it going in the wrong direction.

**Ran out of credits during execution.** FAUNA will notify you if credits run out. Add more credits to your account and try again - FAUNA will remember what you were working on.

* * *

_Last updated: March 2026_

# Techniques | FLORA Docs

Techniques are pre-built, multi-step AI workflows that you can add to your canvas and run with a single click. Each technique encapsulates a complex generation pipeline—combining multiple models and processing steps—into a simple node with defined inputs and outputs.

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------

Instead of manually building complex workflows from scratch, Techniques let you leverage proven creative pipelines built by FLORA and the community. Think of them as "recipes" for AI generation—you provide the ingredients (inputs), and the technique handles all the intermediate steps to produce the final result.

**What makes Techniques powerful:**

*   **Multi-step workflows** - Chain multiple AI models together (e.g., analyze image → generate prompt → create video)
    
*   **Consistent results** - Same pipeline, same quality, every time
    
*   **Time-saving** - Skip the setup and get straight to creating
    
*   **Curated quality** - Each technique is tested and optimized for its specific use case
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#the-techniques-library)

The Techniques Library


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#browsing-techniques)

Browsing Techniques

Access the Techniques Library from the sidebar to explore all available techniques. The library features:

*   **Featured carousel** - Highlighted techniques at the top
    
*   **Category filters** - Browse by use case
    
*   **Search** - Find techniques by name, description, or tags
    
*   **Preview cards** - See sample outputs before adding to canvas
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#categories)

Categories

Techniques are organized into the following categories:

Category

Description

Brand & Visual Design

Logo treatments, brand assets, visual identity

Product Visualization

Product shots, mockups, lifestyle imagery

Marketing & Ads

Ad creatives, social media content, campaigns

Video & Animation

Motion graphics, animated sequences, video ads

Fashion & Apparel Editorial

Lookbooks, fashion photography, styling

Content Packaging

Thumbnails, covers, promotional materials

Print Film/VFX

Film-quality effects, cinematic treatments

Space & Architecture

Interior design, architectural visualization

Fun & Inspiration

Creative experiments, artistic styles

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#technique-details)

Technique Details

Click any technique card to view its detail page, which shows:

*   **Description** - What the technique does and ideal use cases
    
*   **Inputs required** - What you need to provide (images, videos, or text)
    
*   **Outputs produced** - What you'll receive when the technique completes
    
*   **Example presets** - Sample inputs and their corresponding outputs
    
*   **Credit cost** - How many credits the technique uses per run
    
*   **Estimated time** - Approximate execution duration
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#adding-techniques-to-your-canvas)

Adding Techniques to Your Canvas


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#from-the-library)

From the Library

1

**Browse and Select**

Open the Techniques Library and find a technique that matches your needs. Click the technique card to view details.

2

**Add to Canvas**

Click the **Add to Canvas** button. A Technique Node node appears on your canvas with all input and output slots ready.

3

**Connect Inputs**

Provide the required inputs by connecting source nodes to each input slot on the technique node.

4

**Run the Technique**

Once all inputs are connected, click **Run** to execute the technique. The workflow processes automatically and creates output nodes when complete.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#the-technique-node)

The Technique Node


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you add a technique to your canvas, it appears as a Technique Node—a specialized node that represents the entire workflow.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#block-structure)

Block Structure

*   **Header** - Displays the technique name, icon, and credit cost
    
*   **Input slots** - Connection points for each required input (left side)
    
*   **Output slots** - Connection points for each output (right side)
    
*   **Run button** - Execute the technique when all inputs are ready
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#input-cards)

Input Cards

Each input slot shows:

*   **Input name** - What type of content is expected
    
*   **Input type** - Image, video, or text indicator
    
*   **Connection status** - Whether an input is connected or missing
    
*   **Thumbnail** - Preview of the connected input (for images/videos)
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#providing-inputs)

Providing Inputs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Techniques require specific inputs to run. There are several ways to provide each input:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#connect-existing-nodes)

Connect Existing Nodes

Drag a connection from any compatible node output to the technique's input slot:

*   **Image inputs** - Connect from Image nodes, uploads, or other image outputs
    
*   **Video inputs** - Connect from Video nodes or video uploads
    
*   **Text inputs** - Connect from Text nodes
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#quick-input-actions)

Quick Input Actions

Right-click an input slot or use the input menu to quickly add content:

Action

Description

Add Preset

Insert a sample input from the technique's examples

Generate

Run the technique and generate outputs

Upload

Upload a file directly to this input

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#using-presets)

Using Presets

Each technique includes example presets—sample inputs that demonstrate the technique's capabilities. Adding a preset creates a static node with the sample content, letting you test the technique immediately.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#running-techniques)

Running Techniques


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#execution-process)

Execution Process

When you run a technique:

1.  **Validation** - FLORA checks all required inputs are connected and valid
    
2.  **Credit check** - Confirms you have sufficient credits for the run
    
3.  **Processing** - The internal workflow executes step by step
    
4.  **Progress tracking** - The technique node shows real-time progress
    
5.  **Output creation** - Result nodes appear connected to the technique's outputs
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#credit-costs)

Credit Costs

Each technique has a fixed credit cost displayed in the header. This cost covers all the internal generation steps—you pay once for the entire workflow, not per internal step.

circle-info

Credits are charged when the technique starts. If a technique fails, credits are automatically refunded.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#progress-indicator)

Progress Indicator

While running, the technique node displays:

*   **Progress bar** - Visual indicator of completion percentage
    
*   **Current step** - Which internal node is currently processing
    
*   **Estimated time remaining** - Approximate time until completion
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#working-with-outputs)

Working with Outputs


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#output-nodes)

Output Nodes

When a technique completes, it automatically creates output nodes on your canvas:

*   **Image outputs** - Appear as result image blocks
    
*   **Video outputs** - Appear as result video blocks
    
*   **Text outputs** - Appear as result text blocks
    

These output nodes are connected to the technique node and can be used as inputs for other nodes in your workflow.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#feedback)

Feedback

After a technique completes, you can provide feedback on the outputs using the thumbs up/down buttons. This helps improve technique quality over time.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#chaining-techniques)

Chaining Techniques

Output nodes from one technique can be connected to inputs of another technique or any other node, enabling complex multi-technique workflows.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#detaching-techniques)

Detaching Techniques


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Want to see how a technique works internally? You can "detach" a technique to expand it into its constituent nodes.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#how-to-detach)

How to Detach

1.  Select the Technique Node
    
2.  Click the **Detach** option in the toolbar or context menu
    
3.  The technique expands into individual nodes on your canvas
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#what-happens)

What Happens

*   The technique node is replaced by all internal nodes
    
*   Connections are preserved and mapped to the expanded nodes
    
*   You can now see and modify each step of the workflow
    

circle-exclamation

Detaching is one-way—you cannot re-collapse nodes back into a technique node. Consider duplicating the technique before detaching if you want to keep the original.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#tips-for-using-techniques)

Tips for Using Techniques


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Check the examples first** - Review technique presets to understand what inputs work best
    
*   **Match input quality** - Higher quality inputs generally produce better outputs
    
*   **Mind aspect ratios** - Some techniques work best with specific aspect ratios (noted in input descriptions)
    
*   **Test with presets** - Try the built-in presets before using your own content
    
*   **Watch credit costs** - Complex techniques with many steps may cost more credits
    
*   **Use technique outputs downstream** - Chain technique outputs into other nodes for extended workflows
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#technique-vs.-manual-workflows)

Technique vs. Manual Workflows


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Aspect

Technique

Manual Workflow

Setup time

Instant—just add and connect inputs

Requires building from scratch

Consistency

Same pipeline every time

May vary between sessions

Customization

Fixed internal workflow

Full control over every parameter

Learning curve

Use immediately without expertise

Requires understanding each model

Credit cost

Single fixed cost

Varies based on nodes used

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#common-use-cases)

Common Use Cases


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Product photography** - Transform product shots into lifestyle imagery
    
*   **Ad creation** - Generate multiple ad variations from a single product image
    
*   **Video production** - Convert static images into animated video content
    
*   **Brand assets** - Create consistent branded materials from reference images
    
*   **Social content** - Produce platform-optimized content from source materials
    
*   **Concept exploration** - Quickly test creative directions without manual setup
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#app-mode)

App Mode


------------------------------------------------------------------------

Techniques can also be run outside of the canvas using App Mode. This provides a streamlined, focused interface where you simply provide inputs and run the technique—no canvas setup required. App Mode is ideal for quick, repeated use of your favorite techniques without the overhead of managing a full project.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques#technique-builder)

Technique Builder


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Technique Builder lets you package any multi-step workflow on your canvas into a reusable Technique — define inputs, define outputs, and publish. You can also edit published Techniques to update their workflow, inputs, outputs, or listing details.

circle-info

For the full guide on creating, editing, and publishing your own Techniques, see [**Technique Builder**](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder)
.

[PreviousBatch Nodechevron-left](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/batch-node)
[NextTechnique Builderchevron-right](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder)

Last updated 8 days ago

# Claude Haiku 3.5 (by Anthropic) | FLORA Docs

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/models/text-models/claude-haiku-3.5-by-anthropic#overview)

Overview

Anthropic’s latency-optimized Claude model for quick drafting and multimodal summaries.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/models/text-models/claude-haiku-3.5-by-anthropic#quick-facts)

Quick facts

*   **Modes:** Text → Text · Image → Text · Video → Text
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/models/text-models/claude-haiku-3.5-by-anthropic#what-its-great-for)

What it’s great for

*   Rapid Q&A and brainstorming with minimal delay
    
*   Generating captions or notes from supplied images
    
*   Converting short clips into concise recaps
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/models/text-models/claude-haiku-3.5-by-anthropic#copy-and-paste-prompts)

Copy-and-paste prompts

Copy

    Answer the customer questions listed in `input_texts` using a friendly tone.

Copy

    Provide descriptive alt text for the attached product lifestyle image.

Copy

    Summarize the key beats from this 30-second walkthrough video.

Copy

    Draft three headline options responding to the feedback in `input_texts`.

Type

Notes

Text

—

Quick drafting, ideation

Captioning, visual notes

# Technique Builder | FLORA Docs

Technique Builder lets you package any multi-step workflow on your canvas into a reusable Technique. Define what goes in, what comes out, and publish it — so you or anyone else can reuse it as a single node on canvas or as a standalone app.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you've ever built a workflow you want to reuse — or share with your team — Technique Builder is how you turn it into a first-class Technique.

**What you can do:**

*   **Compress workflows** — Collapse a multi-node pipeline into a single reusable step
    
*   **Publish to your Workspace** — Make it available in the Techniques Library for your team
    
*   **Reuse anywhere** — Drop your published Technique onto any canvas like a regular node
    
*   **Share as an app** — Others can run your Technique through a simplified app interface, no canvas required
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#getting-started)

Getting Started


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To open Technique Builder, click the **Build Technique** button at the bottom of the canvas. This button appears when you have a workflow on your canvas that's ready to be packaged.

circle-info

When you enter Technique Builder mode, your canvas nodes become **locked for editing**. This is by design — the builder needs a stable snapshot of your workflow to define inputs and outputs. You can exit at any time to resume editing.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#the-builder-flow)

The Builder Flow


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Technique Builder walks you through four steps:

Step

What you do

**Intro**

Learn what Technique Builder does and how it works

**Input**

Select which nodes serve as inputs to your Technique

**Output**

Select which nodes serve as outputs of your Technique

**Publish**

Fill in details and publish your Technique

A progress bar at the top of the panel tracks your current step. You can navigate back to previous steps at any time.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#step-1-intro)

Step 1: Intro


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The intro screen gives you a quick walkthrough of what Technique Builder enables:

1.  **Compress your creative workflow into a single step**
    
2.  **Publish it to the Workspace library**
    
3.  **Reuse it anywhere on canvas**
    
4.  **Share with others as a simple app**
    

Click **Start Building** to begin defining your Technique's inputs and outputs.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#step-2-define-inputs)

Step 2: Define Inputs


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**"What should be the inputs?"**

Select the nodes on your canvas that should serve as the inputs to your Technique. Inputs are what the user provides when they run the Technique — for example, a reference image, a text prompt, or a style image.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#how-input-selection-works)

How input selection works

When you're on the Input step, **click nodes directly on the canvas** to select them as inputs. A node qualifies as an input candidate if:

*   It has **no incoming connections** (i.e., it's a starting node in your workflow)
    
*   It has **generated output content** (an image, video, or text result)
    
*   It's a **supported node type** (standard generation nodes — not groups, comments, layer editors, collections, or technique nodes)
    

Selected inputs appear as cards in the builder panel. You must select **at least one input** to continue.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#configuring-each-input)

Configuring each input

For each selected input, you can customize:

*   **Name** — Give the input a clear, descriptive label (e.g., "Reference Photo", "Style Prompt"). This is what users will see when running your Technique. Names are required and must not be empty.
    
*   **Description** (optional) — A short explanation of what this input expects (max 40 characters). This helps users understand what to provide.
    
*   **Preset** — A preview of the current content on this node. When someone uses your Technique, this content serves as the default/example value.
    

To remove an input, click the trash icon on its card.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#step-3-define-outputs)

Step 3: Define Outputs


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**"What should be the outputs?"**

Select the nodes on your canvas that represent the final results of your workflow. Outputs are what the Technique produces — the generated images, videos, or text that users will receive.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#how-output-selection-works)

How output selection works

Click nodes on the canvas to select them as outputs. A node qualifies as an output candidate if:

*   It has **no outgoing connections** (i.e., it's an end node in your workflow)
    
*   It has **generated output content**
    
*   It's a **supported node type**
    

You must select **at least one output** to continue.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#configuring-each-output)

Configuring each output

Output cards work the same as input cards:

*   **Name** — A descriptive label for the output (e.g., "Final Render", "Upscaled Video")
    
*   **Description** (optional) — What this output produces (max 40 characters)
    
*   **Preset** — A preview thumbnail of the current output content
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#graph-validation)

Graph validation

When you click **Continue** from the outputs step, the builder validates your Technique's graph to ensure it's well-formed. Validation checks include:

*   All inputs and outputs are properly connected
    
*   No circular dependencies exist in the workflow
    
*   All referenced nodes have valid configurations
    
*   Node types are compatible with the Technique format
    

If validation fails, you'll see an error message explaining what needs to be fixed before you can proceed.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#step-4-publish)

Step 4: Publish


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**"Publish your Technique"**

Review your Technique and fill in the details that help others discover, understand, and use it.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#name)

Name

The name of your Technique as it will appear in the library and on canvas.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#description)

Description

A description of what this Technique generates and how to use it (max 200 characters). This appears as a subtitle in the library. Name and description are both required to publish.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#credit-cost)

Credit Cost

The total credit cost to run your Technique, automatically calculated from the models and generation steps in your workflow. This is displayed to users before they run the Technique.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#thumbnail)

Thumbnail

A preview image for your Technique in the library. The builder automatically generates a thumbnail from your output nodes, but you can upload a custom one by clicking **Upload**.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#category-optional)

Category (optional)

Assign your Technique to a category so users can find it when browsing the library:

Category

Best for

Brand & Visual Design

Logo, brand identity, and visual design workflows

Product Visualization

Product shots, mockups, and 3D renders

Marketing & Ads

Ad creatives, campaign assets, and promotional content

Video & Animation

Video generation, animation, and motion graphics

Fashion & Apparel Editorial

Fashion shoots, lookbooks, and apparel visualization

Content Packaging

Social media, thumbnails, and content formatting

Film & VFX

Film production, VFX, and cinematic content

Space & Architecture

Interior design, architecture, and spatial design

Fun & Inspiration

Creative experiments and artistic exploration

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#tags-optional)

Tags (optional)

Add keyword tags to improve discoverability (e.g., `marketing`, `ads`, `film`). Type a tag and press **Enter**, **Tab**, or use a comma to add it. You can also paste multiple comma-separated tags at once. Remove tags by clicking the **x** on each badge.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#app-link)

App Link

A preview of the shareable URL for your Technique: `flora.ai/technique/your-technique-name`. The slug is automatically generated from the Technique name.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#visibility)

Visibility

Control who can access your Technique:

Visibility

Access

Status

**Unlisted**

Only people with the link can find it

Available

**Public**

Anyone with the link can access

Coming soon

**Workspace**

Everyone in your workspace can access

Coming soon

**Private**

Only you can access

Coming soon

Currently, **Unlisted** is the only available visibility option. Public, Workspace, and Private visibility options are coming soon.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#publishing)

Publishing


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once you've filled in a name, description, and selected a visibility option, click **Publish** to create your Technique.

After publishing:

*   Your Technique appears in the Workspace Techniques Library
    
*   Others can add it to their canvas from the library
    
*   It's accessible via its app link for use outside the canvas
    
*   A confirmation toast confirms the publish was successful
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#editing-a-published-technique)

Editing a Published Technique


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

After publishing, you can edit your Technique to update its workflow, inputs, outputs, or listing details. Editing updates the existing Technique in place — it doesn't create a separate copy.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#how-to-start-editing)

How to start editing

Hover over a Technique node on your canvas to reveal its toolbar. If you're the Technique's creator, you'll see an **Edit technique** button (pencil icon). Click it to enter edit mode.

When you enter edit mode, the Technique node is **detached** — its internal workflow is expanded back onto your canvas as individual nodes inside a group, so you can modify them directly. A snapshot of the original state is saved so your changes can be reverted if you cancel.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#the-edit-flow)

The edit flow

Editing walks you through four steps, shown in a progress bar at the top of the panel:

Step

What you do

**Workflow**

Edit prompts, update nodes, connect or disconnect nodes

**Input**

Review and update which nodes serve as inputs

**Output**

Review and update which nodes serve as outputs

**Publish**

Update listing details (name, description, thumbnail, etc.) and republish

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#step-1-edit-workflow)

Step 1: Edit Workflow

Your Technique's workflow is expanded onto the canvas. The canvas is unlocked during this step — you can:

*   Edit prompts and model parameters on any node
    
*   Change models on generation nodes
    
*   Add or remove nodes from the workflow
    
*   Connect or disconnect nodes to restructure the pipeline
    

Click **Continue** when you're done editing the workflow to proceed to input selection.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#steps-2-4-input-output-publish)

Steps 2–4: Input, Output, Publish

These steps work the same as when creating a new Technique. The builder pre-populates your previous input/output selections and listing details, so you only need to adjust what's changed.

When you click **Publish**, the existing Technique is updated. Anyone using it will get the new version the next time they run it.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#cancelling-an-edit)

Cancelling an edit

Click **Cancel** or the **X** button at any time to discard your changes. The canvas reverts to its original state — the detached nodes are removed and the original Technique node is restored with its previous connections.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#toolbar-actions)

Toolbar actions

The Technique node toolbar also provides:

*   **Detach into nodes** — Expands the Technique into individual canvas nodes without entering edit mode. Useful for forking a Technique into a standalone workflow.
    
*   **View workflow** — Opens a read-only overlay showing the Technique's internal workflow graph.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#tips-and-best-practices)

Tips & Best Practices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Run your workflow first** — Make sure all nodes have generated outputs before entering Technique Builder. Nodes without output content can't be selected as inputs or outputs.
    
*   **Use clear names** — Input and output names are what users see when running your Technique. Be specific: "Product Photo" is better than "Input 1".
    
*   **Keep descriptions short** — You have 40 characters. Focus on what the user needs to know: "Upload a front-facing product shot" tells them exactly what to provide.
    
*   **Choose meaningful outputs** — Select the final, polished results — not intermediate steps. Users expect the output to be the finished product.
    
*   **Test before publishing** — Ensure your workflow produces consistent, high-quality results before packaging it as a Technique.
    
*   **Pick the right category** — Correct categorization helps users find your Technique when browsing the library.
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#supported-and-unsupported-node-types)

Supported & Unsupported Node Types


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Not all node types can be used as inputs or outputs in a Technique. Here's what's supported:

**Supported as inputs/outputs:**

*   Image nodes (text-to-image, image-to-image)
    
*   Video nodes (text-to-video, image-to-video)
    
*   Text nodes (text-to-text, image-to-text, video-to-text)
    
*   Static image blocks
    
*   Empty image blocks
    

**Not supported as inputs/outputs:**

*   Collection nodes
    
*   Comments
    
*   Groups
    
*   Layer Editor nodes
    
*   Inpaint/Outpaint image blocks
    
*   Result blocks (image, text, video)
    
*   Technique nodes (nested techniques)
    

circle-exclamation

**Intermediate nodes are preserved.** Nodes that sit between your selected inputs and outputs are automatically included in the Technique graph — you don't need to select them. The builder traces the connections from outputs back to inputs and retains all nodes along the path.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/technique-builder#exiting-the-builder)

Exiting the Builder


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can exit Technique Builder at any time by clicking the **X** button in the panel header or clicking **Go Back** on the intro screen. If you have unsaved changes (selected inputs/outputs or publish details), you'll be asked to confirm before discarding your draft.

[PreviousTechniqueschevron-left](https://docs.flora.ai/nodes/techniques)
[NextEditorchevron-right](https://docs.flora.ai/editor/editor)

Prompt tips

*   Be explicit about length and format (bullets, code block, JSON).
    
*   Provide context and relevant assets for best results.
    
*   Use for complex multi-step reasoning tasks.

# Community | FLORA Docs

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/more/community#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------

FLORA's community is a dynamic ecosystem where creativity, collaboration, and innovation thrive. It brings together a diverse group of artists, designers, technologists, and thinkers who share a passion for exploring the intersection of technology and art. Our community is a space for constant growth, experimentation, and inspiration.

From creative systems to interactive design techniques, these workflows are meant to inspire and empower you to push your creative boundaries. We've curated professional creative workflows in several categories: **Popular**, **Concepting**, **Design**, **Marketing**, **Moving Image**, **Experimental.**

# Common Use Cases / FAQs | FLORA Docs

chevron-rightIs there a way to export a video at more than 24 FPS?[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../common-use-cases-faqs#is-there-a-way-to-export-a-video-at-more-than-24-fps)

Yes - you can connect your videos to another video node and use the Topaz Upscaler, which offers an FPS (frames per second) parameter. Set the parameters on the sidebar to whatever value you are looking for.

![](https://docs.flora.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F526296967-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWthH0GpcCHwVdtbvahZS%252Fuploads%252F5SIx1pgihDkeOVdJzpXE%252Fimage%2520%2848%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D431cc2f1-edc9-4660-ba93-36de5e064922&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b51a581e&sv=2)

chevron-rightWhat's the maximum file size for uploading to Flora?[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../common-use-cases-faqs#whats-the-maximum-file-size-for-uploading-to-flora)

The upload limit is 350mb for images, but model providers often have lower ceilings.

# Credit Refunds | FLORA Docs

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#failed-generations)

Failed Generations


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sometimes generations don't go as planned. If you experience a failed generation—where credits were deducted but you didn't receive usable output—we're here to help.

**Common causes of failed generations:**

*   Server timeouts or connectivity issues
    
*   Model errors or unexpected failures
    
*   Incomplete or corrupted outputs
    
*   Generation stuck in processing
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#how-to-request-a-refund)

How to Request a Refund


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you believe credits were incorrectly deducted due to a failed generation:

1.  Email us at [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://docs.flora.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e3909693938c9197a3858f8c91828582968d82cd828a)
    
2.  Include your **project URL** (found in your browser's address bar)
    
3.  Briefly describe what happened (e.g., "Image generation failed with error message")
    

Our team will review your request and investigate the issue. If we confirm a failed generation, we'll refund the credits to your account.

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#what-to-expect)

What to Expect


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Response time:** We typically respond within 1-2 business days
    
*   **Investigation:** We'll review the generation logs associated with your project
    
*   **Resolution:** Approved refunds are credited back to your account
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#tips-to-avoid-failed-generations)

Tips to Avoid Failed Generations


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Ensure a stable internet connection during generation
    
*   Avoid closing the browser tab while a generation is in progress
    
*   For long-running generations (like video), keep the tab active
    

* * *

For any billing questions, reach out to [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://docs.flora.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#92e1e7e2e2fde0e6d2f4fefde0f3f4f3e7fcf3bcf3fb)

[PreviousManage Subscriptionchevron-left](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../manage-subscription)
[NextCommon Use Cases / FAQschevron-right](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../common-use-cases-faqs)

Last updated 1 month ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Failed Generations](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#failed-generations)
    
*   [How to Request a Refund](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#how-to-request-a-refund)
    
*   [What to Expect](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#what-to-expect)
    
*   [Tips to Avoid Failed Generations](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds#tips-to-avoid-failed-generations)

# Manage Subscription | FLORA Docs

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../manage-subscription#subscription-cancellation)

Subscription Cancellation


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**How to Cancel**

You can cancel your subscription at any time:

1.  From the home page, go to your **workspace** page.
    
2.  Click the **settings icon** (gear) in the workspace header.
    

![Settings icon](https://docs.flora.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F526296967-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWthH0GpcCHwVdtbvahZS%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-8f262252cafc938a63ee89e35da422e0381e2dc1%252Fsettings-icon.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fb889378&sv=2)

1.  In the sidebar, select **People and Credits**.
    

![People and Credits](https://docs.flora.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F526296967-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWthH0GpcCHwVdtbvahZS%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-4339104b778de98c77347050294ab4b7354cc2e6%252Fpeople-and-credits.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5e6a326&sv=2)

1.  On the People & Credits page, click the **Manage** button (next to "Next billing").
    

![Manage button](https://docs.flora.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F526296967-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWthH0GpcCHwVdtbvahZS%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-f60b5e2871eeca0ae83e96f2ec448a7e4346f187%252Fmanage-button.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=88125625&sv=2)

1.  In Stripe, update or cancel your subscription (e.g. click **Cancel Subscription** and follow the steps).
    

> **Note:** If your latest payment failed (Past Due), the Cancel button may be hidden by the billing portal. Please contact [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.flora.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#75060005051a07013513191a07141314001b145b141c)
>  to resolve this.

**After Cancellation**

*   Your plan stays active until the end of the current billing cycle
    
*   You retain full access to all models during that time
    
*   Your credits still remain in your account (while active, [unused subscription credits roll over each billing cycle](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#unused-credits)
     with no limits)
    
*   Your subscription won’t renew automatically
    
*   We don’t issue partial refunds for unused time
    

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../manage-subscription#refund)

Refund


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All payments are final and non-refundable, unless FLORA approves an exception.

Refunds may be granted in cases such as:

*   Duplicate charges
    
*   Billing errors
    
*   Other exceptional situations, at FLORA’s sole discretion
    

If approved, refunds will be issued to the original payment method.

* * *

For billing support, email us at [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://docs.flora.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#0d7e787d7d627f794d6b61627f6c6b6c78636c236c64)

[PreviousUnsplashchevron-left](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../unsplash)
[NextCredit Refundschevron-right](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../credit-refunds)

Last updated 28 days ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Subscription Cancellation](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../manage-subscription#subscription-cancellation)
    
*   [Refund](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../manage-subscription#refund)
    

Was this helpful?

# Usage-Based Pricing | FLORA Docs

This doc explains how our pricing changes in January 2026 affect your existing subscription and what options you have moving forward.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#your-current-plan-is-grandfathered)

Your Current Plan is Grandfathered

If you're already a FLORA subscriber, your current plan and pricing remain unchanged. Here's what this means:

*   Your existing subscription continues at your current rate indefinitely
    
*   You'll keep the same number of seats and credit allocation
    
*   No automatic migrations or forced upgrades will occur
    
*   Your billing date and payment method remain the same
    

You can continue using your current plan for as long as you'd like. There's no deadline or expiration on this protection.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#whats-improving-for-everyone)

What's Improving for Everyone

Alongside the pricing changes, we're making improvements that apply to all users—including those on grandfathered plans:

*   **All models now available to everyone:** Every AI model in FLORA is accessible on every plan, including free
    
*   **All features unlocked:** Downloads, exports, and other previously gated features are now available to all users
    
*   **Free tier expanded:** Free accounts now receive 1,000 credits to explore FLORA
    

These changes take effect immediately, regardless of which plan you're on.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#understanding-your-current-plan-vs.-new-pricing)

Understanding Your Current Plan vs. New Pricing

Your current plan uses seat-based pricing, where each seat comes with a fixed credit allocation. The new model eliminates seats entirely—you purchase a credit pool that your whole team shares.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#example-current-seat-based-plan)

Example: Current Seat-Based Plan

Let's say your team currently has 3 Pro seats:

*   Cost: 3 seats × $20/seat = $60/month
    
*   Credits: 3 seats × 20,000 credits = 60,000 credits total
    
*   Access: Only those 3 seat-holders can use FLORA
    

If you wanted to add a 4th team member, you'd pay an additional $20/month for another seat.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#example-new-credit-pooled-pricing)

Example: New Credit-Pooled Pricing

Under the new structure, that same team would look like this:

*   Cost: $54/month (Studio plan) for 60,000 credits
    
*   Access: **Unlimited** team members share the credit pool
    
*   Adding people: No additional cost—invite as many as you need
    

For teams that need more credits, volume discounts and annual billing provide additional savings:

**Plan**

**Monthly**

**Annual (per month)**

**Starter (20K credits)**

$18

$17

**Studio (60K credits)**

$54

$45

**Scale (250K credits)**

$200

$187.50

The larger your team, the more you save—because you're no longer paying per person.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#unused-credits)

Unused credits

Subscription credits refresh each billing cycle, and unused credits roll over month to month with no limits—we don't take them away at the end of a period. Credit packs (one-time purchases) never expire and remain in your account until used.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#what-triggers-a-switch-to-new-pricing)

What Triggers a Switch to New Pricing

Your grandfathered plan remains active until you decide to access the billing portal and select a new plan.

Important: Any plan modification is a one-way door. Once you're on the new pricing, you cannot return to your grandfathered plan.

If you're happy with your current setup, you don't need to do anything. Your plan will continue unchanged.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#should-you-switch)

Should You Switch?

Consider switching to the new pricing if:

*   You want to add team members without paying per seat
    
*   Your team size fluctuates and you'd benefit from flexible access
    
*   You're ready to scale and want better rates on larger credit purchases
    

Consider staying on your current plan if:

*   You're a solo user and your current allocation meets your needs
    
*   Your team size is stable and you don't anticipate adding people
    
*   You prefer the predictability of your existing setup
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../usage-based-pricing#questions-or-need-help)

Questions or Need Help?

If you'd like help understanding which option works best for your situation:

*   Email: [\[email protected\]](https://docs.flora.ai/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
    
*   Enterprise customers: Contact your account manager directly
    

We're committed to making this transition as smooth as possible. Your work shouldn't be disrupted by billing changes.

# Workspaces | FLORA Docs

Workspaces are how FLORA organizes your projects, team members, and credits. Each workspace has its own plan, credit balance, and team — so it's important to make sure you're in the right one.

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#switching-workspaces)

Switching Workspaces


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click the **workspace selector** in the top-left corner of the dashboard. It shows your current workspace's logo, name, and member count.

The dropdown displays all workspaces you belong to, along with each workspace's **plan type** and **member count**. Your active workspace has a checkmark next to it. If you've been invited to a workspace you haven't joined yet, it will appear here with a **Join** button.

To switch, click any workspace in the list. FLORA remembers the last workspace you used, so you'll land there automatically next time you log in.

> **Tip:** If you belong to many workspaces, use the search bar at the top of the dropdown to find the one you need.

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#checking-your-credits)

Checking Your Credits


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Your credit balance is specific to the workspace you're currently in. To see it in the sidebar, enable the **Show Credit Balance** toggle in your **Preferences** — your remaining credits will then appear in the bottom-left of the sidebar next to the flower icon (e.g. "5.2K").

![The Preferences panel with the Show Credit Balance toggle enabled](https://docs.flora.ai/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F526296967-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWthH0GpcCHwVdtbvahZS%252Fuploads%252Fgit-blob-7d72ba1a4cbe865603d7f6f42a32446729330d24%252Fpreferences-show-credit-balance.png%3Falt%3Dmedia&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef00cc31&sv=2)

For a full breakdown, open your workspace settings and go to **People & Credits**. This page shows:

*   **Credit Plan** — your current plan name and credits per billing period
    
*   **Credits Remaining** — your available balance, with an option to add more credits (admin only)
    
*   **Next Billing** — your next billing date and amount, with a **Manage** button to open your Stripe billing portal (admin only)
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#why-do-i-see-0-credits)

Why do I see 0 credits?

This is almost always because you're viewing the wrong workspace. If your plan is active and you see 0 credits:

1.  Click the **workspace selector** in the top-left corner.
    
2.  Look for the workspace that has your active plan (check the plan type shown next to each workspace name).
    
3.  Switch to that workspace — your credits will appear in the sidebar and under People & Credits.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#creating-a-workspace)

Creating a Workspace


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To create a new workspace, click the **workspace selector** and select **Create a new workspace** at the bottom. The setup has three steps:

1.  **Name** — choose a name for your workspace (minimum 3 characters).
    
2.  **Plan** — select a billing plan.
    
3.  **Invite team** — optionally invite team members by email. You can skip this step and invite people later.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#inviting-team-members)

Inviting Team Members


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Make sure you're in the correct workspace before inviting anyone. You can invite from two places:

*   The **member count badge** in the top-right of the dashboard
    
*   The **Invite** button on the People & Credits page
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#invite-methods)

Invite methods

*   **Email** — enter one or more email addresses (separated by commas, semicolons, or spaces), choose a role, and send.
    
*   **Link** — copy a shareable invite link. You can choose between an **edit link** or a **view link**.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#roles)

Roles

Role

Label

Permissions

Admin

Admin

Full permissions — manage billing, settings, and all workspace features. Can invite admins, editors, and guests.

Editor

Can edit

Can edit projects and invite editors and guests. Cannot manage billing.

Guest

Can view

View-only access. Cannot edit projects or invite others.

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../workspaces#workspace-settings)

Workspace Settings


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To access workspace settings, click the **settings icon** (gear) in the workspace header. Admin-only settings include:

*   **Rename workspace** — edit the workspace name directly.
    
*   **Upload logo** — click the workspace avatar to upload a custom image.
    
*   **Model Access Control** — choose whether new AI models are available by default (opt-out) or must be manually enabled (opt-in), with per-model toggles.
    

Any member can **leave a workspace** from the settings page, as long as it's not their only workspace.

> **Note:** Workspaces cannot be deleted. If you no longer need a workspace, you can leave it.

[PreviousHiggsfield DoP (by Higgsfield)chevron-left](https://docs.flora.ai/models/video-models/higgsfield-dop-by-higgsfield)
[NextStyles (deprecated)chevron-right](https://docs.flora.ai/faqs-how-to.../styles)

# Data, Security, & IP | FLORA Docs

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/legal/data-security-and-ip#inputs)

Inputs

You retain full ownership and confidentiality over all assets you upload. None of your uploaded files, prompts, or related metadata are used to train or fine-tune models — either by FLORA or by any of our infrastructure or model partners. We operate under strict “no-training” agreements with all enterprise-grade API vendors.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/legal/data-security-and-ip#outputs)

Outputs

You own the rights to all generated outputs created in your account. There are no usage or commercial limitations tied to plan tiers. For clarity: FLORA and its partners do not claim any rights to your generated outputs.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/legal/data-security-and-ip#training-and-api-agreements)

Training & API Agreements

No input, output, or prompt data are shared with upstream providers for model improvement. Enterprise workspaces include default “no-training” and DPA (Data Processing Addendum) coverage across all models used through FLORA. These protections also apply to Agency and Pro workspaces that handle client data.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/legal/data-security-and-ip#upstream-vendors)

Upstream Vendors

If an upstream provider updates its terms, FLORA reviews and enforces alignment with our data-protection policy before adoption. We only integrate with vendors that support enterprise-grade data isolation and IP protection.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.flora.ai/legal/data-security-and-ip#plan-differences)

Plan Differences

There are no IP ownership or data-use differences between Free, Pro, Agency, and Enterprise tiers — the main differences are around capacity, collaboration, and support. Enterprise plans include SSO (Single Sign-On) and additional legal documentation (DPA, SOC-2, etc.) for teams that require formal compliance and security assurance.

We take data integrity seriously and are committed to ensuring creative and client work remains private, protected, and exclusively yours.

Read more about our privacy policy and terms of service [herearrow-up-right](https://flora.ai/legal/privacy-policy)
.

[PreviousEducationchevron-left](https://docs.flora.ai/more/education)
